Weekly expenses (for example grosseries), monthly expenses (like rent), quaterly expenses (once per 3 months) and annual expenses (yearly). \r\nOnce a book month has been created for the next month, that month is usable as a account ledger. You can also create loops with [ and ]. The loop starts if the value of the current cell is greater than 0, and ends if the cell that is pointed at the end of it is 0. If the source code contains characters that are not the Brainf*ck operators, they are ignored by the interpreter, so you can write your comments inside the code without any problems. \r\n\r\n// You
